doWithAds = function(inside, failureMessage){
if ('consoleLog' in window &&
'generic' in window &&
'ad_utils' in window &&
'custom' in window &&
'monitoring' in generic &&
'document_is_ready' in generic) {
try{
inside.call(this);
}catch(e) {
if ( window.ueLogError ) {
if(typeof failureMessage !== 'undefined'){
e.message = failureMessage;
}
e.attribution = "Advertising";
e.logLevel = "ERROR";
ueLogError(e);
}
if( (document.location.hash.match('debug=1')) &&
(typeof failureMessage !== 'undefined') ){
console.error(failureMessage);
}
}
} else {
if( (document.location.hash.match('debug=1')) &&
(typeof failureMessage !== 'undefined') ){
console.error(failureMessage);
}
}
};

rel="login">Edit</a>
    </span>
    
        <h2>Storyline</h2>
        
        <div class="inline canwrap">
            <p>
                <span>    With many people fearing the actions of super heroes, the government decides to push for the Hero Registration Act, a law that limits a hero's actions. This results in a division in The Avengers. Iron Man stands with this Act, claiming that their actions must be kept in check otherwise cities will continue to be destroyed, but Captain America feels that saving the world is daring enough and that they cannot rely on the government to protect the world. This escalates into an all-out war between Team Iron Man (Iron Man, Black Panther, Vision, Black Widow, War Machine, and Spider-Man) and Team Captain America (Captain America, Bucky Barnes, Falcon, Scarlet Witch, Hawkeye, and Ant Man) while a new villain emerges.</span>
                <em class="nobr">Written by
<a href="/search/title?plot_author=RespectTheHyphen&view=simple&sort=alpha&ref_=tt_stry_pl"
>RespectTheHyphen</a></em>            </p>
        </div>

        <h2>Did You Know?</h2>
    <div id="trivia" class="txt-block">
        <h4>Trivia</h4>
    In the comics, while Spider-Man started off on Iron Man's side, he later shifted over to Captain America's side after learning that the Pro-Registration Side was imprisoning the captured unregistered heroes in a prison built in another dimension known as the "Negative Zone", against their will, without due process (as it is technically not on American soil) until they agreed to register. In this movie, he fights on Iron Man's side, before being sent home by Iron Man after the battle at the airport in Germany.        <a href="trivia?ref_=tt_trv_trv"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>
                <hr />
     <div id="goofs"  class="txt-block">
        <h4>Goofs</h4>
During the opening scene, set in 1991, the computer monitors surrounding Winter Soldier do not appear to be of that year. However, previous installments have shown that secret societies such as SHIELD and HYDRA have access to technologies which the rest of the world doesn&#39;t have yet.        <a href="trivia?tab=gf&ref_=tt_trv_gf"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>   
                <hr />

    <div class="article" id="titleUserReviewsTeaser">
        <h2>User Reviews</h2>
        <div class="user-comments">
                    <div class="tinystarbar" title="8/10">
                        <div style="width: 80px;">&nbsp;</div>
                    </div>
                <span>
                    <strong>Infinity War is in good hands.</strong>
                    <div class="comment-meta">
                        13 April 2016 | by <a href="/user/ur27874480/?ref_=tt_urv"
><span>areebkhan619</span></a>
                        &ndash; <a href="/user/ur27874480/comments?ref_=tt_urv"
>See all my reviews</a>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <p>Checkmate, haters. And sorry, it&#39;s just not your year. I have seen this movie, but I won&#39;t mention a single spoiler here. (If you guys want proof, you can PM me and I&#39;ll tell you how the movie ends and the after credits). The reason I&#39;m really writing this review is that I KNOW THERE WILL BE BIASED PEOPLE HERE WHO&#39;LL WRITE THAT BVS IS BETTER and this is trash, etc, etc. Well, just see this movie and judge for yourself. Speaking briefly of the movie, it is an emotional roller coaster with an absolutely beautiful end. Spidey had a satisfying screen time. As for the acting, by the time the movie ended, I was a happy man. Russov&#39;s are handling Infinity War, and after watching this movie, how they did justice to characters, I&#39;ll not worry. A movie we wanted as well as deserve.</p>
                    </div>
                </span>
